***депо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:депо.html>депо́</a> (9318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed in the 18th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dépôt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:депо.html>депо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">depó, dɛpó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> depot, station, warehouse (company or facility that provides maintenance, repair and parking for rolling stock, usually rail)</li>
<li>station, firehouse, fire station (facility that accommodates fire trucks and special equipment)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожарный.html>пожа́рное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:депо.html>депо́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">požárnoe depó, požárnoe dɛpó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">депо́вец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">depóvec, dɛpóvec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деревенский.html>дереве́нский</a> (2913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">derévnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревенский.html>дереве́нский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">derevénskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>country, rural, rustic; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> village
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:деревенский.html>дереве́нская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>derevénskaja</b> žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>rural</b> life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:деревенский.html>дереве́нский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдых.html>о́тдых</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>derevénskij</b> ótdyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vacationing in a <b>rural</b> area</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***деревня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a> (620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьrvьňa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*Dr̥Hweh₂</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">druva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cornfield, plough-land</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">dirvà</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">field, land</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">dirvónas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fallow field, set-aside land</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Baltic borrowing (with later semantic change from plough-land to homestead and then to hamlet) is likely considering the lack of cognates in other Slavic languages.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">derévnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дереве́нь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>village, hamlet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the countryside, the rural population</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> both feminine and masculine with animacy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yokel, bumpkin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пиджак.html>пиджа́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смокинг.html>смо́кинг</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Derévnja</b>! Éto ne pidžák, éto smóking.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a yokel! This isn't a coat, it’s a tuxedo.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a>? — <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a>? — <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужи́к</a> […] — <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a>? […] <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>поса́дит</a>?! <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:памятник.html>па́мятник</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sidít? — Kto? — Nu, mužík […] — O <b>derévnja</b>, a? […] Kto ž jevó posádit?! On že pámjatnik!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Is he sitting? — Who? — That man. — Bumpkin! Who could throw him in prison? He’s a monument! (Play on the meanings of <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a>, meaning to sit and to be in prison, in the movie, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gentlemen_of_Fortune" class="extiw" title="w:Gentlemen of Fortune">Gentlemen of Fortune</a>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Traditionally, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">derévnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> referred to a smaller village without a church, while <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>село́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">seló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> referred to a larger village with a church.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">village</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поселок.html>посёлок</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">posjólok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поселение.html>поселе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poselénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>село</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">selo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:селение.html>селе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">selénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́ца</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">staníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хутор.html>ху́тор</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xútor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">yokel</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дереве́нщина</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">derevénščina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревенский.html>дереве́нский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">derevénskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рев.html>ре́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня</b>

***дерево.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дерево</a> (454)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dervo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dóru</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tree</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>дре́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drévo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dérevo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рева</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́вья</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дерева́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́вьев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́в</a><sup>*</sup></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дерёв</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Obsolete.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<dl><dd><i>Note: the irregular soft ending of this plural was originally used to form feminine collective nouns.</i></dd></dl>
<ol><li>tree
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каучуковый.html>каучу́ковое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kaučúkovoje <b>dérevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">rubber tree</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">каме́дное <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kamédnoje <b>dérevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gum tree, sweet gum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лиственный.html>ли́ственное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lístvennoje <b>dérevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">foliage tree</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвойный.html>хво́йное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xvójnoje <b>dérevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">conifer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wood (only <i>singular</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">де́рево-ка́мень</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dérevo-kámenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">petrified wood</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krásnoje <b>dérevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mahogany</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čórnoje <b>dérevo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ebony</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резьба.html>резьба́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́реву</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rezʹbá po <b>dérevu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">woodcutting, wood engraving</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***деревянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деревянный.html>деревя́нный</a> (1195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">деревѧнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">derevęnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dervěnъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*derwēno-</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*derwoyno-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*deru-</i> (see <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dóru</i>). Morphologically <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dervo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ěnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деревянный.html>деревя́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">derevjánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wood; wooden</li>
<li>woody, ligneous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:деревянный.html>деревя́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>derevjánnoje</b> máslo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lamp oil, low-grade olive oil</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>woody</b> oil</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дьржава</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dĭržava</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="defdate">[1344]</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьržava</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strength; estate; state <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">government</span><span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">дзяржа́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dzjaržáva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">дрьжава</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drĭžava</span><span tr Latn">drŭžava</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">държа́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dǎržáva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">state <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">government</span><span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держава.html>держа́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">deržáva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держава.html>держа́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держава.html>держа́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>state, power</li>
<li>orb, globe, mound</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́вший</a> (348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***держать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a> (348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьržati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hold, to support</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">deržátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подержать.html>подержа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сдержа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hold, to keep, to support
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹ</b> pri sebé kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to keep</b> somebody close by oneself, <b>to keep</b> somebody around</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹ</b> pri sebé štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to keep</b> something to oneself, <b>to hold</b> something inside</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹ</b> kovó-libo za rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to hold</b> somebody by the hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹ</b> drug drúga za rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to hold</b> hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹ</b> sebjá v rukáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have control over oneself, to keep oneself in hand, to keep oneself under control</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пазуха.html>па́зухой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо / <a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹ</b> kámenʹ za pázuxoj na kovó-libo / prótiv kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to harbor a grudge towards someone /against someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дер.html>дер</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:подержать.html>подержа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сдержа́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-держ-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a> (921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">deržátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подержаться.html>подержа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hold on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>ма́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> а́нна <b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máša i Ánna <b>deržálisʹ</b> za rúki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Masha and Anna <b>held</b> their hands.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перила.html>пери́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> za períla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold on to the banister / rail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold (by, to), to stick (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тема.html>те́мы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> témy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stick to the subject</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to conduct / comport oneself, to behave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызывающий.html>вызыва́юще</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:наглый.html>на́гло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> vyzyvájušče/náglo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to outface</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to keep, to stick (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:левый.html>ле́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> lévoj storoný</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep (to the) left</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>бе́рега</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> bérega</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hug the shore</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вместе.html>вме́сте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> vméste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold / stick / keep together</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороне́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> v storoné</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stand aside / aloof, to keep / hold aloof</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прямо.html>пря́мо</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> prjámo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stand up straight, to hold oneself erect / upright</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold out, to stand firm; to hold one's ground
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держи́сь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržísʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">steady!, stand firm! (<i>don't give up</i>); hold tight</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продержаться.html>продержа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proderžátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to restrain oneself, to bear up</li>
<li>to last
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">takóje položénije ne móžet dólgo <b>deržátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this state of affairs cannot last long</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продержаться.html>продержа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proderžátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: to be held up (by), to be supported (by)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ниточка.html>ни́точке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>deržátʹsja</b> na nítočke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hang by a thread</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерзать.html>дерза́ть</a> (28134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьrzati</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерзить.html>дерзи́ть</a> (26636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***дерзкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерзкий.html>де́рзкий</a> (7162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьrzъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерзкий.html>де́рзкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dérzkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)де́рзче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brazen, impudent, impertinent, insolent, cheeky, pert</li>
<li>bold, daring, audacious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерзкий.html>де́рзко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dérzko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b>де́рз<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3*a/c. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a>  |  <i>дерзей, дерзее</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дерз-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>са́нт</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
